               \n                    Katie Moulton                \n            \n                                    Last year, Conor Oberst returned to his home town of Omaha after more than a decade in New York. While there, he got to work recording an album, but the resulting powerful yet downright barren recordings on last fall’s Ruminations were only intended as demos.
